# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
a matrix made of all 0 ^a23W41dS

multiply each number in the matrix by that multiple ^RiTPiD52

you multiply the columns of the second for the rows of the first,
you also sum the results. The columns of the first needs to be as many as the
rows of the second, also it is not commutative, AB is not the same as BA ^LWNBuly2

multiply a matrix by itself, as easy as that ^kz8H9UeZ

The matrix has to be a square matrix, else the comlu ^Wp1geAtR
